# Pell 方程 - OI Wiki

- Source: https://oi-wiki.org/math/number-theory/pell-equation/

# Pell 方程

前置知识：[连分数](../continued-fraction/)、[二次域](../quadratic/)

## 引入

本文讨论（广义）Pell 方程的求解．广义 Pell 方程是指关于 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的不定方程

𝑥2−𝐷𝑦2=𝑁,x2−Dy2=N,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

其中，𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是正整数且不是完全平方数1，𝑁N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是非零整数．狭义的 Pell 方程特指 𝑁 =1N=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 或 𝑁 = ±1N=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的特殊情形，有时也包括 𝑁 = ±4N=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形．广义 Pell 方程与在实二次整数环内寻找范数为 𝑁N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次整数紧密相关，而常常称作（狭义）Pell 方程的这些情形可以看作是寻找实二次整数环内的单位数．

当本文提及 Pell 方程时，特指 𝑁 =1N=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形．相应地，𝑁 = −1N=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形称为负 Pell 方程2（negative Pell's equation）．

## 解的结构

广义 Pell 方程的整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和二次整数 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 联系密切，因此文献中 Pell 方程的解常常写作 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的形式．因为二次整数的范数

𝑁(𝑥+𝑦√𝐷)=𝑥2−𝐷𝑦2,N(x+yD)=x2−Dy2,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

所以，广义 Pell 方程大致相当于在求解范数为 𝑁N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次整数．但是，两者确实有细微的区别．当 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是整数时，𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定是二次整数；反过来，二次整数未必要求 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是整数——在 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 还可以同时是半整数3．

这个区别在求解基本单位数时格外重要．因为二次整环中的单位数是指范数为 ±1±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次整数．对于 𝐷 ≡2,3(mod4)D≡2,3(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，要找到这样的单位数，只需要求解广义 Pell 方程在 𝑁 = ±1N=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形即可；但是对于 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，还需要考虑 𝑁 = ±4N=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形．下文 会讨论单位数的求解方法．

要理解广义 Pell 方程解的结构，需要从 [Brahmagupta 恒等式](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brahmagupta%27s_identity) 入手：

(𝑥21−𝐷𝑦21)(𝑥22−𝐷𝑦22)=(𝑥1𝑥2+𝐷𝑦1𝑦2)2−𝐷(𝑥1𝑦2+𝑥2𝑦1)2.(x12−Dy12)(x22−Dy22)=(x1x2+Dy1y2)2−D(x1y2+x2y1)2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

它相当于二次整数的范数保持乘法，即

𝑁(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷)𝑁(𝑥2+𝑦2√𝐷)=𝑁((𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷)(𝑥2+𝑦2√𝐷))=𝑁((𝑥1𝑥2+𝐷𝑦1𝑦2)+(𝑥1𝑦2+𝑥2𝑦1)√𝐷).N(x1+y1D)N(x2+y2D)=N((x1+y1D)(x2+y2D))=N((x1x2+Dy1y2)+(x1y2+x2y1)D).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

利用这一恒等式，可以利用方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁1x2−Dy2=N1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁2x2−Dy2=N2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解复合出方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁1𝑁2x2−Dy2=N1N2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解．当然，从二次整数的角度看，解的复合就是二次整数的乘法，这就体现了将 Pell 方程的解记作二次整数形式的方便之处．特别地，取 𝑁1 =𝑁N1=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑁2 =1N2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就可以发现，如果已知 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的一组解和相应的 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的全体解，就可以得到 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 更多的解．当然，这种方法未必能够生成全部的解．但是，这至少说明理解 Pell 方程的解的结构对理解广义 Pell 方程的解的结构有重要作用．

### Pell 方程

方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的几何意义是实轴在 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴、虚轴在 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴的双曲线．双曲线上的每个点都唯一对应了 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的一个非零取值：双曲线的左支对应着 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的负值，右支则对应正值．而且，在每一支上，双曲线自下而上对应的 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的取值是严格递增的．二次整数的取值给 Pell 方程的解赋予了自然的顺序．

双曲线同时关于 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴和 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴对称，因此讨论 Pell 方程的解只需要考虑在第一象限内的那一段即可，其余解可以通过对称性获得．这相当于只考虑 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷 >1x+yD>1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．如果方程除了 ( ±1,0)(±1,0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之外还存在不平凡的解，那么一定在第一象限内存在 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 取值最小的解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，这也是第一象限内（不含坐标轴）横纵坐标都最小的整点，它称为 Pell 方程的基本解（fundamental solution）4．根据前文的讨论，满足 𝑥𝑘 +𝑦𝑘√𝐷 =(𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷)𝑘xk+ykD=(x1+y1D)k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数对 (𝑥𝑘,𝑦𝑘)(xk,yk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是 Pell 方程的解，而且都在第一象限．反过来，这也的确是 Pell 方程在第一象限内的全部解．再利用对称性，就可以得到如下结论：

定理

设 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解是 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．那么，它的全部解就是

{(𝑥,𝑦):𝑥+𝑦√𝐷=±(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷)𝑘,𝑘∈𝐙}.{(x,y):x+yD=±(x1+y1D)k,k∈Z}.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)证明

首先证明第一象限中不存在其他解．不妨设存在其他解 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且对于某个 𝑘 ≥0k≥0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有

𝑥𝑘+𝑦𝑘√𝐷<𝑥+𝑦√𝐷<𝑥𝑘+1+𝑦𝑘+1√𝐷.xk+ykD<x+yD<xk+1+yk+1D.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

几何意义上，这相当于说整点 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 落入了双曲线上 (𝑥𝑘,𝑦𝑘)(xk,yk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (𝑥𝑘+1,𝑦𝑘+1)(xk+1,yk+1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之间（不含端点）．将不等式同时乘以 𝑥𝑘 −𝑦𝑘√𝐷 =(𝑥𝑘 +𝑦𝑘√𝐷)−1xk−ykD=(xk+ykD)−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就得到

1<(𝑥+𝑦√𝐷)(𝑥𝑘−𝑦𝑘√𝐷)=(𝑥𝑥𝑘−𝐷𝑦𝑦𝑘)+(𝑥𝑘𝑦−𝑥𝑦𝑘)√𝐷<𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷.1<(x+yD)(xk−ykD)=(xxk−Dyyk)+(xky−xyk)D<x1+y1D.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

根据前文提到的单调性，这个不等式就说明 (𝑥𝑥𝑘 −𝐷𝑦𝑦𝑘,𝑥𝑘𝑦 −𝑥𝑦𝑘)(xxk−Dyyk,xky−xyk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是位于 (1,0)(1,0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之间的整点．这与 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的选取矛盾．

将第一象限的解扩展到整个平面时，指数 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 取相反数（即整体取倒数）就是关于 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴对称，整体取相反数则是关于原点对称．再加上 𝑘 =0k=0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时的平凡解，就得到 Pell 方程的全部解．

前文的讨论只是假设了基本解的存在．现在要说明的是，Pell 方程总是存在非平凡的解．

定理

Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 总是存在除了 ( ±1,0)(±1,0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之外的整数解．

证明

首先，[Dirichlet 定理](../continued-fraction/#用渐近分数逼近实数) 表明存在无数对正整数 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得

∣𝑥𝑦−√𝐷∣≤1𝑦2|xy−D|≤1y2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

成立，它们都满足不等式

|𝑥2−𝐷𝑦2|=𝑦2∣𝑥𝑦−√𝐷∣∣𝑥𝑦+√𝐷∣≤1𝑦2+2√𝐷<1+2√𝐷.|x2−Dy2|=y2|xy−D||xy+D|≤1y2+2D<1+2D.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

因而，必然存在整数 𝑚 ∈( −1 −2√𝐷,1 +2√𝐷)m∈(−1−2D,1+2D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得有无数对 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都满足 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑚x2−Dy2=m![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．将这些 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 根据对 𝑚m![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的余数分类，就知道对某一对整数 (𝑥0,𝑦0)(x0,y0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，一定存在无数对 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得 𝑥 ≡𝑥0(mod𝑚)x≡x0(modm)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 以及 𝑦 ≡𝑦0(mod𝑚)y≡y0(modm)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 成立．任取满足这些条件的两对互异的 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，则

𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷𝑥2+𝑦2√𝐷=𝑥1𝑥2−𝐷𝑦1𝑦2𝑚+𝑥2𝑦1−𝑥1𝑦2𝑚√𝐷.x1+y1Dx2+y2D=x1x2−Dy1y2m+x2y1−x1y2mD.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

因为根据同余关系有

𝑥1𝑥2−𝐷𝑦1𝑦2≡𝑥20−𝐷𝑦20=𝑚≡0(mod|𝑚|),𝑥2𝑦1−𝑥1𝑦2≡𝑥0𝑦0−𝑥0𝑦0=0(mod|𝑚|),x1x2−Dy1y2≡x02−Dy02=m≡0(mod|m|),x2y1−x1y2≡x0y0−x0y0=0(mod|m|),![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

这说明上式右侧得到的是整数解．而且，因为 (𝑥1,𝑦1) ≠(𝑥2,𝑦2)(x1,y1)≠(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，它并不平凡．这就说明 Pell 方程的确存在非平凡解．

当然，本节提供的是非构造性的证明，在下文讨论 Pell 方程的解法时，会直接利用连分数的渐近分数构造出 Pell 方程的解，因而提供了 Pell 方程存在非平凡解的另一种证明．另外，尽管本节得到的 Pell 方程解的结构与实二次整数环的单位数的结构是一致的，但是对于 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，本节并没有完全解决相应的二次整数环的单位数的结构问题，下文将进一步讨论．

### 广义 Pell 方程

广义 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的图像同样是平面上的双曲线，同样以 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴和 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴为对称轴．前文已经指出，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的部分解可能只相差一个 Pell 方程解的因子，这意味着可以将方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解划分为等价类．对于方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的两个解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，如果存在 Pell 方程的解 (𝑢,𝑣)(u,v)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得 𝑥2 +𝑦2√𝐷 =(𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷)(𝑢 +𝑣√𝐷)x2+y2D=(x1+y1D)(u+vD)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 成立，那么称解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 等价．两个解等价的充分必要条件是

𝑁∣(𝑥1𝑥2−𝐷𝑦1𝑦2), 𝑁∣(𝑥2𝑦1−𝑥1𝑦2).N∣(x1x2−Dy1y2), N∣(x2y1−x1y2).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

因为 Pell 方程的解相对容易求出，一个自然的想法是在上述的每个等价类中各求出一个解．只要知道这些解，就可以利用相应的 Pell 方程的解得到所要求的广义 Pell 方程的全部解．在广义 Pell 方程的解的等价类中，由于对称性，每个等价类都存在纵坐标 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 非负但是尽可能小的解：如果这样的解唯一，它就称为该等价类的基本解；否则，该等价类必然有两个 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 非负且最小的解，而且它们关于 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 轴对称，此时选择 𝑥 >0x>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的那个作为基本解．由此，求解广义 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，就相当于求解它的基本解集 𝑈U![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．设它对应的 Pell 方程的基本解是 (𝑟,𝑠)(r,s)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，则广义 Pell 方程的全部解的集合是

{(𝑥,𝑦):𝑥+𝑦√𝐷=±(𝑟+𝑠√𝐷)𝑘(𝑢+𝑣√𝐷),𝑘∈𝐙,𝑢+𝑣√𝐷∈𝑈}.{(x,y):x+yD=±(r+sD)k(u+vD),k∈Z,u+vD∈U}.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

广义 Pell 方程的基本解必然是有限的．这是因为从上面的通解表达式可知，绝对值 |𝑢 +𝑣√𝐷||u+vD|![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 必然位于 𝑟 −𝑠√𝐷r−sD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑟 +𝑠√𝐷r+sD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之间．文末的参考文献中提供了关于基本解的坐标的范围的更严格的估计．当然，与 Pell 方程的情形不同，广义 Pell 方程可能没有解．

利用广义 Pell 方程的一个解 (𝑢,𝑣)(u,v)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 Pell 方程的基本解 (𝑟,𝑠)(r,s)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 得到同一个等价类中的全部解的方法，除了利用解的复合之外，还可以利用如下递推关系

𝑥𝑘=2𝑟𝑥𝑘−1−𝑥𝑘−2, 𝑦𝑘=2𝑟𝑦𝑘−1−𝑦𝑘−2,xk=2rxk−1−xk−2, yk=2ryk−1−yk−2,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

其中，𝑥𝑘 +𝑦𝑘√𝐷 =(𝑟 +𝑠√𝐷)𝑘(𝑢 +𝑣√𝐷)xk+ykD=(r+sD)k(u+vD)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．这是因为 𝑥𝑛xn![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦𝑛yn![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都可以对某一对实数 (𝐴,𝐵)(A,B)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 写成 𝐴(𝑟 +𝑠√𝐷)𝑘 +𝐵(𝑟 −𝑠√𝐷)𝑘A(r+sD)k+B(r−sD)k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的形式，而根据 Vieta 定理，𝑟 ±𝑠√𝐷r±sD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −2𝑟𝑥 +1 =0x2−2rx+1=0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的两个实根，进而 𝑥𝑛xn![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦𝑛yn![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都满足上述的二阶常系数递推关系．相较于解的复合，该递推公式有更少的乘法次数．

## 求解方法

Pell 方程和广义 Pell 方程的求解都可以基于连分数进行．

### PQa 算法

本文讨论的算法都基于 PQa 算法，它可以用于求出特定的二次无理数的连分数展开．

设整数 𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷P0,Q0,D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 满足 𝑄0 ≠0Q0≠0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝐷 >0D>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且不是完全平方数，以及 𝑃20 ≡𝐷(mod𝑄0)P02≡D(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．那么，二次无理数

𝜔=𝑃0+√𝐷𝑄0ω=P0+DQ0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

的连分数展开 [𝑎0,𝑎1,⋯][a0,a1,⋯]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 可以通过如下 [递推公式](../continued-fraction/#二次无理数) 求得：

𝑎𝑘=⌊𝑃𝑘+√𝐷𝑄𝑘⌋, 𝑃𝑘+1=𝑎𝑘𝑄𝑘−𝑃𝑘, 𝑄𝑘+1=𝐷−𝑃2𝑘+1𝑄𝑘.ak=⌊Pk+DQk⌋, Pk+1=akQk−Pk, Qk+1=D−Pk+12Qk.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

进而，𝜔ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的第 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个渐近分数的分子和分母 𝐴𝑘Ak![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝐵𝑘Bk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 由如下 [递推公式](../continued-fraction/#递推关系) 给出：

𝐴𝑘=𝑎𝑘𝐴𝑘−1+𝐴𝑘−2, 𝐵𝑘=𝑎𝑘𝐵𝑘−1+𝐵𝑘−2Ak=akAk−1+Ak−2, Bk=akBk−1+Bk−2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

且 𝐴−1 =1A−1=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝐴−2 =0A−2=0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝐵−1 =0B−1=0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝐵−2 =1B−2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

这些公式的正确性已经在连分数一文中得到证明．那里也说明了，因为二次无理数是 [循环连分数](../continued-fraction/#二次无理数)，所以，三元组 (𝑃𝑘,𝑄𝑘,𝑎𝑘)(Pk,Qk,ak)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 最终将进入循环，算法总可以在有限步内终止．不妨设循环节的最小长度是 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，且循环的最早的起始位置是 𝑘0k0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，则二次无理数的连分数展开可以写作

𝜔=[𝑎0,⋯,𝑎𝑘0−1,―――――――𝑎𝑘0,⋯,𝑎𝑘0+ℓ−1].ω=[a0,⋯,ak0−1,ak0,⋯,ak0+ℓ−1―].![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

利用 PQa 算法解决 Pell 方程，需要建立如下结论：

定理

继续上述记号．设 𝐺𝑘 =𝑄0𝐴𝑘 −𝑃0𝐵𝑘Gk=Q0Ak−P0Bk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，则整数对 (𝐺𝑘−1,𝐵𝑘−1)(Gk−1,Bk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 满足关系式

𝐺2𝑘−1−𝐷𝐵2𝑘−1=(−1)𝑘𝑄0𝑄𝑘,Gk−12−DBk−12=(−1)kQ0Qk,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

且它们的最大公因数 gcd(𝐺𝑘−1,𝐵𝑘−1)gcd(Gk−1,Bk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 整除 𝑄𝑘Qk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

证明

设 𝜔ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的连分数展开中，第 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个余项（完全商）为 𝜔𝑘ωk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，即

𝜔=[𝑎0,𝑎1,⋯,𝑎𝑘−1,𝜔𝑘]=𝜔𝑘𝐴𝑘−1+𝐴𝑘−2𝜔𝑘𝐵𝑘−1+𝐵𝑘−2.ω=[a0,a1,⋯,ak−1,ωk]=ωkAk−1+Ak−2ωkBk−1+Bk−2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

将 𝜔 =(𝑃0 +√𝐷)/𝑄0ω=(P0+D)/Q0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝜔𝑘 =(𝑃𝑘 +√𝐷)/𝑄𝑘ωk=(Pk+D)/Qk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 代入上式，就得到

𝑃0+√𝐷𝑄0=(𝑃𝑘+√𝐷)𝐴𝑘−1+𝑄𝑘𝐴𝑘−2(𝑃𝑘+√𝐷)𝐵𝑘−1+𝑄𝑘𝐵𝑘−2.P0+DQ0=(Pk+D)Ak−1+QkAk−2(Pk+D)Bk−1+QkBk−2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

消去左右两侧的分母并比较有理部分和无理部分的系数，再代入 𝐺𝑘Gk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的表达式，就得到如下等式：

𝐺𝑘−1=𝑃𝑘𝐵𝑘−1+𝑄𝑘𝐵𝑘−2,𝐷𝐵𝑘−1=𝑃𝑘𝐺𝑘−1+𝑄𝑘𝐺𝑘−2.Gk−1=PkBk−1+QkBk−2,DBk−1=PkGk−1+QkGk−2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

因此，将一式乘以 𝐺𝑘−1Gk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 减去二式乘以 𝐵𝑘−1Bk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，就有

𝐺2𝑘−1−𝐷𝐵2𝑘−1=(𝐵𝑘−2𝐺𝑘−1−𝐵𝑘−1𝐺𝑘−2)𝑄𝑘=(𝐴𝑘−1𝐵𝑘−2−𝐵𝑘−1𝐴𝑘−2)𝑄0𝑄𝑘=(−1)𝑘𝑄0𝑄𝑘.Gk−12−DBk−12=(Bk−2Gk−1−Bk−1Gk−2)Qk=(Ak−1Bk−2−Bk−1Ak−2)Q0Qk=(−1)kQ0Qk.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

最后一步利用了渐近分数的 [差分公式](../continued-fraction/#误差估计)．这就证明了第一个结论．

为了证明第二个结论，将 𝐺𝑘Gk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的表达式代入第一个结论，有

(𝑄0𝐴𝑘−1−𝑃0𝐵𝑘−1)2−𝐷𝐵2𝑘−1=(−1)𝑘𝑄0𝑄𝑘.(Q0Ak−1−P0Bk−1)2−DBk−12=(−1)kQ0Qk.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

所以，利用 𝑄0 ∣(𝑃20 −𝐷)Q0∣(P02−D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有

𝑄0𝐴2𝑘−1+(𝑃20−𝐷𝑄0𝐵𝑘−1−2𝑃0𝐴𝑘−1)𝐵𝑘−1=(−1)𝑘𝑄𝑘.Q0Ak−12+(P02−DQ0Bk−1−2P0Ak−1)Bk−1=(−1)kQk.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

故而，gcd(𝐺𝑘−1,𝐵𝑘−1) =gcd(𝑄0𝐴𝑘−1,𝐵𝑘−1)gcd(Gk−1,Bk−1)=gcd(Q0Ak−1,Bk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 整除 𝑄𝑘Qk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

这个结论提供了一种寻找方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解的方法．如果合理地选择 𝑄0 >0Q0>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 并选择 𝑃0P0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为同余方程 𝑃20 ≡𝐷(mod𝑄0)P02≡D(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，那么通过对 (𝑃0 +√𝐷)/𝑄0(P0+D)/Q0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 执行 PQa 算法，直到找到 ( −1)𝑘𝑄0𝑄𝑘 =𝑁(−1)kQ0Qk=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，此时 (𝐺𝑘−1,𝐵𝑘−1)(Gk−1,Bk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就成为原方程的一组解．而且，如果 𝑄𝑘 = ±1Qk=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么这样得到的解一定是本原解，也就是说 𝐺𝑘−1Gk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝐵𝑘−1Bk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定是互素的．

这个思想是解决 Pell 方程和广义 Pell 方程的核心．理解了这一思想后，下面就着手处理算法的一些细节，并证明所有的解都可以通过该方式得到．

### Pell 方程

要解决 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，只需要对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(0,1,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(0,1,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法，直到出现 ( −1)𝑘𝑄𝑘 =1(−1)kQk=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，此时 (𝐴𝑘−1,𝐵𝑘−1)(Ak−1,Bk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是 Pell 方程的一组解（因为 𝐺𝑘−1Gk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 此时就是 𝐴𝑘−1Ak−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7))．当然，对于 Pell 方程，对该过程可以进行更精确的描述．

首先，解一定出现在循环节的末尾处．上述过程相当于对 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 做连分数展开．对此，已经有 [结论](../continued-fraction/#纯循环连分数)：

√𝐷=[⌊√𝐷⌋,―――――――――𝑎1,⋯,𝑎ℓ−1,2⌊√𝐷⌋].D=[⌊D⌋,a1,⋯,aℓ−1,2⌊D⌋―].![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

此处，循环节长度为 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，且起始位置是第 11![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 项（下标从 00![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 开始）．而且，它的第 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 项余项等于 ⌊√𝐷⌋ +√𝐷⌊D⌋+D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，这说明 𝑄ℓ =1Qℓ=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因此，如果 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，那么 (𝐴ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Aℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是 Pell 方程的一组非平凡解；如果 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数，那么 (𝐴2ℓ−1,𝐵2ℓ−1)(A2ℓ−1,B2ℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是 Pell 方程的一组非平凡解．

接下来要说明，刚刚得到的这组解一定是基础解．这个结论基于两点理由：第一，Pell 方程的所有正整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 对应的分数 𝑥/𝑦x/y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都出现在 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数中，这就保证了 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 必定是 PQa 算法过程中的某个 (𝐴𝑘,𝐵𝑘)(Ak,Bk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)；第二，除了循环节末尾，不会再出现其他位置有 𝑄𝑘 =1Qk=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，因为 𝐴𝑘Ak![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝐵𝑘Bk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的递推关系保证了它们的大小随着下标增加而增加，所以最小的正整数解（即基础解）必然出现在刚刚指明的位置．这两点理由可以分别从如下的两条定理得出：

定理

设方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有正整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，如果 |𝑁| <√𝐷|N|<D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么 𝑥𝑦xy![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定等于 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数．

证明

当 𝑁 >0N>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，因为 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 >0x2−Dy2>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以 𝑥 >𝑦√𝐷x>yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．故而，有

∣𝑥𝑦−√𝐷∣=𝑁𝑦(𝑥+𝑦√𝐷)<𝑁2𝑦2√𝐷<12𝑦2.|xy−D|=Ny(x+yD)<N2y2D<12y2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

根据 [Legendre 判别法](../continued-fraction/#渐近分数的判定) 可知，𝑥𝑦xy![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数．

当 𝑁 <0N<0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，𝑥 >𝑦√𝐷x>yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不再成立．所以，转而考虑方程 𝑦2 −1𝐷𝑥2 = −𝑁𝐷y2−1Dx2=−ND![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．因为 |𝑁|𝐷 <√1𝐷|N|D<1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以上面的论证依然成立．这说明 𝑦𝑥yx![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 1√𝐷1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数．根据 [倒数定理](../continued-fraction/#递推关系) 可知，𝑥𝑦xy![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 也是 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数．

定理

在对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(0,1,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(0,1,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行上述 PQa 算法的过程中，𝑄𝑘 =1Qk=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 必然推出 ℓ ∣𝑘ℓ∣k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

证明

在 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的连分数展开中，除了第 00![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个余项，所有其他余项都是 [纯循环连分数](../continued-fraction/#纯循环连分数)．设 𝑄𝑘 =1Qk=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．根据 Galois 的结论，必然有余项 𝜔𝑘 =𝑃𝑘 +√𝐷 >1ωk=Pk+D>1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，且它的共轭 −1 <𝑃𝑘 −√𝐷 <0−1<Pk−D<0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，这说明 𝑃𝑘 =⌊√𝐷⌋Pk=⌊D⌋![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因此，余项 𝜔𝑘ωk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就等于 𝜔ℓωℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．但是，余项的重复意味着连分数的循环，如果 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不是 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数倍，就与 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是最小正周期相矛盾．所以，必然有 ℓ ∣𝑘ℓ∣k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

综合本节的讨论可知，只要对 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 做连分数展开，亦即以 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(0,1,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(0,1,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为起点做 PQa 算法，当首次得到 𝑄ℓ =1Qℓ=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，就到达了第一个循环节的末尾．此时，如果 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，那么 (𝐴ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Aℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是 Pell 方程的基本解；否则，(𝐴2ℓ−1,𝐵2ℓ−1)(A2ℓ−1,B2ℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 Pell 方程的基本解．对于循环节长度 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为奇数的情形，并不需要继续 PQa 算法到两倍的循环节处，马上就会说明 𝐴2ℓ−1 +𝐵2ℓ−1√𝐷 =(𝐴ℓ−1 +𝐵ℓ−1√𝐷)2A2ℓ−1+B2ℓ−1D=(Aℓ−1+Bℓ−1D)2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，因而可以直接从 (𝐴ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Aℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 直接计算出 Pell 方程的基本解．Pell 方程所有其他解都可以通过 Pell 方程的基本解计算．

示例

  1. 求解方程 𝑥2 −14𝑦2 =1x2−14y2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(0,1,14)(P0,Q0,D)=(0,1,14)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法结果如下：（标红部分为第一个循环节）

𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑃P![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑄Q![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑎a![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝐴A![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝐵B![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝐺G![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝐺2 −𝐷𝐵2G2−DB2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

(32+5√41)2=2049+320√41.(32+541)2=2049+32041.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

### 负 Pell 方程

根据上一节的讨论可知，负 Pell 方程的解也必然对应于 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数，而且只能出现在 ( −1)𝑘𝑄𝑘 = −1(−1)kQk=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 处．这只能出现在循环节的末尾．因此，负 Pell 方程有解，当且仅当循环节长度 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数．当解存在时，(𝐴ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Aℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是负 Pell 方程的基本解．它的求解方法和上一节是一致的．

利用前文对于 Pell 方程解的结构的证明相仿的思路，可以证明如下结论：

定理

设方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解，且基本解是 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．那么，𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有整数解都属于集合

{(𝑥,𝑦):𝑥+𝑦√𝐷=±(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷)𝑘,𝑘∈𝐙}.{(x,y):x+yD=±(x1+y1D)k,k∈Z}.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

特别地，满足 𝑥2 +𝑦2√𝐷 =(𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷)2x2+y2D=(x1+y1D)2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 正是 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解．

证明

由于对称性，只需要考虑正整数解，即 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷 >1x+yD>1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形．但是由于 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是两段双曲线，所以 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 无法和 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 建立一一对应．为了处理这种困难，首先证明上述的 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解．

显然，(𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．如果设 (𝑧,𝑤)(z,w)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解，那么必然有 1 <𝑧 +𝑤√𝐷 ≤𝑥2 +𝑦2√𝐷1<z+wD≤x2+y2D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．如果右侧的不等式不含有等号，那么将不等式同除以 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就得到 −𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷 <(𝑧 +𝑤√𝐷)( −𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷) <𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷−x1+y1D<(z+wD)(−x1+y1D)<x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．将该不等式的中间项的表达式展开就能得到 𝑥′ +𝑦′√𝐷x′+y′D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的形式，它的范数是 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 (𝑥′,𝑦′)(x′,y′)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 也是整数解．将该不等式取倒数，就发现 −𝑥′ +𝑦′√𝐷−x′+y′D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 同样落入 −𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷−x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之间．二次整数 ±𝑥′ +𝑦′√𝐷±x′+y′D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 互为倒数，必然有一个大于 11![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．但是 11![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不应该再出现别的范数为 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次整数，这与 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小性矛盾．所以，必然成立 𝑥2 +𝑦2√𝐷 =𝑧 +𝑤√𝐷x2+y2D=z+wD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，即 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解．

基于此，如果出现方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不对应某个 (𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷)𝑘(x1+y1D)k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么必然存在 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得 (𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷)2𝑘 <𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷 <(𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷)2𝑘+2(x1+y1D)2k<x+yD<(x1+y1D)2k+2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，消去因子 (𝑥1 +𝑦1)2𝑘+1(x1+y1)2k+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，就说明存在位于 −𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷−x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之间的范数为 ±1±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次整数 𝑥′ +𝑦′√𝐷 ≠1x′+y′D≠1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．重复上一段利用倒数的论证可知，这与 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小性矛盾．因而原命题得证．

因为 (𝐴ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Aℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是负 Pell 方程的最小正整数解，而 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有正整数解都出现在集合

{(𝑥,𝑦):𝑥+𝑦√𝐷=(𝐴ℓ−1+𝐵ℓ−1√𝐷)𝑘,𝑘∈𝐍+}{(x,y):x+yD=(Aℓ−1+Bℓ−1D)k,k∈N+}![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

中，又因为这些正整数解必然对应 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的在循环节末尾（前一位）处的渐近分数，而且渐近分数的分子和分母是严格单调递增的，所以对所有 𝑘 ∈𝐍+k∈N+![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 总是有

(𝐴ℓ−1+𝐵ℓ−1√𝐷)𝑘=𝐴𝑘ℓ−1+𝐵𝑘ℓ−1√𝐷.(Aℓ−1+Bℓ−1D)k=Akℓ−1+Bkℓ−1D.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

在所有这些正整数解中，𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为奇数时就是负 Pell 方程的解，𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为偶数时就是 Pell 方程的解，两者交替出现．

判断负 Pell 方程是否有解，需要计算 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 连分数展开的循环节的长度，这并不容易计算，因此希望能够找到更简单的判断方法．但是，目前并没有条件简明、容易计算的判断方法5．此处仅仅提供一个简单的结论．

定理

方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解，则 44![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不能整除 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不含有 4𝑘 +34k+3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 型的素因子．反过来，如果 𝐷 =2D=2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 或 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 4𝑘 +14k+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 型的素数，那么方程必然有解．

证明

首先，负 Pell 方程有解，就意味着 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次剩余，因而 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 也是 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的任意一个因子 𝑑d![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次剩余，故而 𝑑 ≠4d≠4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝑑d![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不是 4𝑘 +34k+3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 型素数．反过来，方程 𝑥2 −2𝑦2 = −1x2−2y2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解有非平凡解 (1,1)(1,1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．剩下的就是 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 4𝑘 +14k+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 型素数的情形．

设 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 4𝑘 +14k+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 型素数，要证明方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解．思路是通过 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解 (𝑢,𝑣)(u,v)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 入手，构造出 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解 (𝛼,𝛽)(α,β)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．如果 𝑢u![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，将 𝑢2 −𝐷𝑣2 =1u2−Dv2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 两侧对 44![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 取模，就得到 𝑣2 ≡ −1(mod4)v2≡−1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，但是 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 并不是模 44![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的二次剩余．这个矛盾说明 𝑢u![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数．考察等式 𝐷𝑣2 =𝑢2 −1 =(𝑢 +1)(𝑢 −1)Dv2=u2−1=(u+1)(u−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因为 𝑢u![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数，所以 gcd(𝑢 +1,𝑢 −1) =gcd(𝑢 +1,2) =2gcd(u+1,u−1)=gcd(u+1,2)=2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．根据这一事实，将 𝐷𝑣2Dv2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的因子分给 𝑢 +1u+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑢 −1u−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，必然一个是 2𝛼22α2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，另一个是 2𝐷𝛽22Dβ2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，其中，𝛼α![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝛽β![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是互素的正整数而且 𝑣 =2𝛼𝛽v=2αβ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．将 𝑢 =𝛼2 +𝐷𝛽2u=α2+Dβ2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑣 =2𝛼𝛽v=2αβ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 代入 𝑢2 −𝐷𝑣2 =1u2−Dv2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就得到 𝛼2 −𝐷𝛽2 = ±1α2−Dβ2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因为 (𝑢,𝑣)(u,v)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 Pell 方程的基本解而且 (𝛼,𝛽)(α,β)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是比 (𝑢,𝑣)(u,v)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 更小的正整数对，这个等式右侧不能是 +1+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，故而只能是 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．这就证明 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 存在解 (𝛼,𝛽)(α,β)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

如果 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是合数，那么不含有 4𝑘 +34k+3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 型素因子且没有平方因子也不能保证方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解，例如 𝑥2 −34𝑦2 = −1x2−34y2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就没有解．

示例

利用上面的示例中的计算结果可知，方程 𝑥2 −14𝑦2 = −1x2−14y2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 无解，且方程 𝑥2 −41𝑦2 = −1x2−41y2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (𝐺2,𝐵2) =(32,5)(G2,B2)=(32,5)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

### 范数为 ±4 的情形

接下来讨论方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．此时，解的性态取决于 𝐷mod4Dmod4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的大小．

有些情形是容易的．如果 𝐷 ≡0(mod4)D≡0(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么 𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，因而 (𝑥/2,𝑦)(x/2,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑢2 −(𝐷/4)𝑣2 = ±1u2−(D/4)v2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．其余的情形，必然有 𝑥,𝑦x,y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 同时是奇数或者同时是偶数．如果 𝑥,𝑦x,y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 同时是奇数，方程两侧对 44![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 取模就得到 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．所以，如果 𝐷 ≡2,3(mod4)D≡2,3(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么 𝑥,𝑦x,y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 只能同时是偶数，因而 (𝑥/2,𝑦/2)(x/2,y/2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑢2 −𝐷𝑣2 = ±1u2−Dv2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．因此，除了 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解都可以通过相应的（负）Pell 方程的解得到．

现在讨论 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，它不能简单地转化为已经解决的情形．为了找到基本解，可以对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(1,2,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(1,2,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 应用 PQa 算法，当首次得到 𝑄ℓ =2Qℓ=2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，就到达了第一个循环节的末尾．如果循环节长度 𝑙l![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，那么 (𝐺ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Gℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =4x2−Dy2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解；否则，(𝐺ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Gℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −4x2−Dy2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基本解．从 (𝐺ℓ−1,𝐵ℓ−1)(Gℓ−1,Bℓ−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 出发，可以得到方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有解：

⎧{ {⎨{ {⎩(𝑥,𝑦):𝑥+𝑦√𝐷2=±(𝐺ℓ−1+𝐵ℓ−1√𝐷2)𝑘,𝑘∈𝐙⎫{ {⎬{ {⎭.{(x,y):x+yD2=±(Gℓ−1+Bℓ−1D2)k,k∈Z}.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

如果循环节长度 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，所有这些都是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =4x2−Dy2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解；否则，当 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数时，(𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −4x2−Dy2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，而当 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数时，(𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =4x2−Dy2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．

这个算法的正确性依赖于如下事实：

定理

设方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有正整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．如果 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么，(𝑥+𝑦)/2𝑦(x+y)/2y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定是 1+√𝐷21+D2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数．

证明

首先注意到，此时 𝑥,𝑦x,y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 必然奇偶性相同，所以 (𝑥 +𝑦)/2(x+y)/2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是整数．如果 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =4x2−Dy2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，那么 𝑥 >𝑦√𝐷 >2𝑦x>yD>2y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以，

∣(𝑥+𝑦)/2𝑦−1+√𝐷2∣=2𝑦(𝑥+𝑦√𝐷)<12𝑦2.|(x+y)/2y−1+D2|=2y(x+yD)<12y2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

根据 [Legendre 判别法](../continued-fraction/#渐近分数的判定) 可知，(𝑥+𝑦)/2𝑦(x+y)/2y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 1+√𝐷21+D2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数．

如果 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −4x2−Dy2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，那么要建立上述不等式，只需要证明 4𝑦 <𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷4y<x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．这至少对于除了 𝐷 =5,13D=5,13![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之外的情形都成立．对于 𝐷 =5,13D=5,13![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，将 𝑥 =√𝐷𝑦2−4x=Dy2−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 代入该不等式可知，它等价于 2(√𝐷 −2)𝑦2 >12(D−2)y2>1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 成立．除了 (𝐷,𝑦) =(5,1)(D,y)=(5,1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之外，该不等式对于所有 𝐷 =5,13D=5,13![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和正整数 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都成立．剩下的就是验证 (𝐷,𝑦) =(5,1)(D,y)=(5,1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，此时，方程 𝑥2 −5𝑦2 = −4x2−5y2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解是 (𝑥,𝑦) =(1,1)(x,y)=(1,1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，需要验证的是 1111![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 1+√52 =[――1]1+52=[1―]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数，而这是显然成立的．

定理

设 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是正整数但不是完全平方数．二次无理数 𝜔 =1+√𝐷2ω=1+D2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的连分数展开具有形式

𝜔=[⌊𝜔⌋,――――――――――𝑎1,⋯,𝑎ℓ−1,2⌊𝜔⌋−1],ω=[⌊ω⌋,a1,⋯,aℓ−1,2⌊ω⌋−1―],![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

其中，ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为循环节长度，且 𝑎𝑘 =𝑎ℓ−𝑘ak=aℓ−k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 对任何 1 <𝑘 <ℓ1<k<ℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都成立．

证明

因为 ⌊𝜔⌋ −1 +𝜔 >1⌊ω⌋−1+ω>1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，而且它的共轭等于 ⌊𝜔⌋ −𝜔⌊ω⌋−ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，位于 −1−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 00![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 之间，所以根据 [Galois 的结论](../continued-fraction/#纯循环连分数) 可知，⌊𝜔⌋ −1 +𝜔⌊ω⌋−1+ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是纯循环连分数，可以写成

⌊𝜔⌋−1+𝜔=[――――――――――2⌊𝜔⌋−1,𝑎1,⋯,𝑎ℓ−1].⌊ω⌋−1+ω=[2⌊ω⌋−1,a1,⋯,aℓ−1―].![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

而 Galois 关于倒数负共轭的结论说明

1𝜔−⌊𝜔⌋=[――――――――――𝑎ℓ−1,⋯,𝑎1,2⌊𝜔⌋−1].1ω−⌊ω⌋=[aℓ−1,⋯,a1,2⌊ω⌋−1―].![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

因此，根据连分数的定义，有

⌊𝜔⌋−1+𝜔=2⌊𝜔⌋−1+11𝜔−⌊𝜔⌋=[2⌊𝜔⌋−1,――――――――――𝑎ℓ−1,⋯,𝑎1,2⌊𝜔⌋−1].⌊ω⌋−1+ω=2⌊ω⌋−1+11ω−⌊ω⌋=[2⌊ω⌋−1,aℓ−1,⋯,a1,2⌊ω⌋−1―].![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

连分数展开的唯一性就说明 𝑎𝑘 =𝑎ℓ−𝑘ak=aℓ−k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 对所有 1 <𝑘 <ℓ1<k<ℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都成立，因而要证明的展开式也成立．

定理

设 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．在对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(1,2,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(1,2,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行上述 PQa 算法的过程中，𝑄𝑘 =2Qk=2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 必然推出 ℓ ∣𝑘ℓ∣k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

证明

在 1+√𝐷21+D2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的连分数展开中，除了第 00![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个余项，所有其他余项都是 [纯循环连分数](../continued-fraction/#纯循环连分数)．设 𝑄𝑘 =2Qk=2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．根据 Galois 的结论，必然有余项 𝜔𝑘 =𝑃𝑘+√𝐷2ωk=Pk+D2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的共轭 −1 <𝑃𝑘−√𝐷2 <0−1<Pk−D2<0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，亦即 √𝐷 −2 <𝑃𝑘 <√𝐷D−2<Pk<D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因为 PQa 算法中总有 𝑄𝑘 ∣𝑃2𝑘 −𝐷Qk∣Pk2−D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)（见 [算法正确性证明](../continued-fraction/#二次无理数)），所以 𝑃𝑘Pk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定是奇数，这就说明 𝑃𝑘Pk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 取值唯一，即 𝑃𝑘 =𝑃0 +2(⌊𝜔⌋ −1)Pk=P0+2(⌊ω⌋−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，也就是说余项 𝜔𝑘 =𝜔ℓωk=ωℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．但是，余项的重复意味着连分数的循环，如果 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不是 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数倍，就与 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是最小正周期相矛盾．所以，必然有 ℓ ∣𝑘ℓ∣k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

定理

设方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．那么，它的全部解就是

⎧{ {⎨{ {⎩(𝑥,𝑦):𝑥+𝑦√𝐷2=±(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2)𝑘,𝑘∈𝐙⎫{ {⎬{ {⎭.{(x,y):x+yD2=±(x1+y1D2)k,k∈Z}.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)证明

根据对称性，只需要考虑正整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 即可．此处需要证明的只有集合中的实数对 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 确实是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解．剩下的事情只需要复述对方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解的结构的证明即可．

实际上要证明的是，对于方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的任何整数解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (𝑥2,𝑦2)(x2,y2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，如下定义的正实数对 (𝑥3,𝑦3)(x3,y3)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 仍然是整数解：

𝑥3+𝑦3√𝐷2=𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2𝑥2+𝑦2√𝐷2.x3+y3D2=x1+y1D2x2+y2D2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

展开右侧，比较有理项和无理项的系数可知

𝑥3=𝑥1𝑥2+𝐷𝑦1𝑦22, 𝑦3=𝑥1𝑦2+𝑥2𝑦12.x3=x1x2+Dy1y22, y3=x1y2+x2y12.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

因为对 𝑖 =1,2i=1,2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有 𝑥𝑖 ≡𝑥2𝑖 ≡𝐷𝑦2𝑖 ≡𝐷𝑦𝑖(mod2)xi≡xi2≡Dyi2≡Dyi(mod2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以

2𝑥3=𝑥1𝑥2+𝐷𝑦1𝑦2≡𝐷2𝑦1𝑦2+𝐷𝑦1𝑦2=𝐷(𝐷+1)𝑦1𝑦2≡0(mod2),2𝑦3=𝑥1𝑦2+𝑥2𝑦1≡𝐷𝑦1𝑦2+𝐷𝑦2𝑦1=2𝐷𝑦1𝑦2≡0(mod2).2x3=x1x2+Dy1y2≡D2y1y2+Dy1y2=D(D+1)y1y2≡0(mod2),2y3=x1y2+x2y1≡Dy1y2+Dy2y1=2Dy1y2≡0(mod2).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

这说明 𝑥3x3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦3y3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是整数．再利用范数保持乘法的性质可知，(𝑥3,𝑦3)(x3,y3)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．

综合这些事实，重复前文几节的论述，就可以说明用于解决方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的上述算法的正确性．这些结果说明，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 具有和方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 类似的简单的解的结构：它的所有解都可以通过其最小正整数解表示出来，而无需求解其它方程．

其实，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有解都可以在方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解中找到，因而从这个角度看，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 更为基础．显然，(𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，当且仅当 (2𝑥,2𝑦)(2x,2y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．前文的分析指出，当 𝐷 ≡2,3(mod4)D≡2,3(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有解都一定同为偶数，因而对应于 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．

当 𝐷 ≡0(mod4)D≡0(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 中，𝑥x![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定是偶数，但是 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 可能是奇数．如果在方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 中，𝑦1y1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数，那么在所有解中 𝑦y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 也一定是偶数，此时这些整数解和方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解一一对应；但是，如果在最小整数解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 中，𝑦1y1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数，那么 𝑦𝑘yk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的奇偶性将和 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一致，交替变化，因而只有当 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数时，才对应于方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．如果 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解中 𝑦1y1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是奇数而且 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的范数是 −4−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么，对于这样的 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −4x2−Dy2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解，但是 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 无解．

当 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 可能同时是奇数，也可能同时是偶数．如果最小正整数解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 已经同时是偶数，那么它的所有整数解也一定同时是偶数，所以总是对应于方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解．如果最小正整数解 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 同时是奇数，那么有如下结论：

定理

设方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解是 (𝑥1,𝑦1)(x1,y1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．如果 𝑥1x1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑦1y1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 同时是奇数，那么，𝐷 ≡5(mod8)D≡5(mod8)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，且该方程的整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 同时是偶数，当且仅当

𝑥+𝑦√𝐷2=±(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2)3𝑘,𝑘∈𝐙.x+yD2=±(x1+y1D2)3k,k∈Z.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)证明

等式 𝑥21 −𝐷𝑦21 = ±4x12−Dy12=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的两边同时对 88![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 取模，得到 𝐷 ≡5(mod8)D≡5(mod8)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．要证明第二个结论，首先证明 (𝑥3,𝑦3)(x3,y3)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是偶数，因为

𝑥3+𝑦3√𝐷2=(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2)3=𝑥31+3𝐷𝑥𝑦218+3𝑥21𝑦1+𝐷𝑦318√𝐷,x3+y3D2=(x1+y1D2)3=x13+3Dxy128+3x12y1+Dy138D,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

所以，只需要证明右侧是整数．因为奇数的平方模 88![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 余 11![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以，有

𝑥31+3𝐷𝑥𝑦1=𝑥1(𝑥21+3𝐷𝑦1)≡𝑥1(1+3×5×1)=16𝑥1=0(mod8),3𝑥21𝑦1+𝐷𝑦31=𝑦1(3𝑥21+𝐷𝑦21)≡𝑦1(3×1+5×1)=8𝑦1=0(mod8).x13+3Dxy1=x1(x12+3Dy1)≡x1(1+3×5×1)=16x1=0(mod8),3x12y1+Dy13=y1(3x12+Dy12)≡y1(3×1+5×1)=8y1=0(mod8).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

这就说明了 𝑥3,𝑦3x3,y3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是偶数．进而，对于所有 𝑘 ∈𝐙k∈Z![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，都有

𝑥+𝑦√𝐷2=±(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2)3𝑘=±(𝑥3+𝑦3√𝐷2)𝑘∈𝐙,x+yD2=±(x1+y1D2)3k=±(x3+y3D2)k∈Z,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

所以此时的 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是偶数．反过来，对于 𝑟 =1,2r=1,2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，总有

±(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2)3𝑘+𝑟=±(𝑥3+𝑦3√𝐷2)𝑘(𝑥𝑟+𝑦𝑟√𝐷2).±(x1+y1D2)3k+r=±(x3+y3D2)k(xr+yrD2).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

要证明相应的 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 不是整数，只需要证明该式不是整数，也就是右侧的乘积中第二项不是整数．这在 𝑟 =1r=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，就是已知条件；在 𝑟 =2r=2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，因为

𝑥2+𝑦2√𝐷2=(𝑥1+𝑦1√𝐷2)2=𝑥21+𝐷𝑦214+𝑥1𝑦12√𝐷,x2+y2D2=(x1+y1D2)2=x12+Dy124+x1y12D,![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

而且 𝑥21 +𝐷𝑦21 ≡1 +1 ×1 =2(mod4)x12+Dy12≡1+1×1=2(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝑥1𝑦1 ≡1(mod2)x1y1≡1(mod2)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以该式也不是整数．这就证明了，只有幂次是 33![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的倍数的时候，相应的解才都属偶数．

也就是说，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的每三个解中就有一个同时是偶数，它对应着 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的整数解．这也说明，对于 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −4x2−Dy2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解，当且仅当方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解．

到目前为止的讨论，已经足够计算实二次整数环的基本单位数．设 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是正整数且不含平方因子．对于 𝐷 ≡2,3(mod4)D≡2,3(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，只需要求出 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±1x2−Dy2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解；而对于 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，只需要求出 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = ±4x2−Dy2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解．当得到最小正整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，对于 𝐷 ≡2,3(mod4)D≡2,3(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，基本单位数就是 ±𝑥 ±𝑦√𝐷±x±yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)；对于 𝐷 ≡1(mod4)D≡1(mod4)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，基本单位数就是 ±𝑥±𝑦√𝐷2±x±yD2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

示例

  1. 求解方程 𝑥2 −14𝑦2 = ±4x2−14y2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

利用前文的示例中的计算可知，方程 𝑥2 −14𝑦2 =4x2−14y2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (30,8)(30,8)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，方程 𝑥2 −14𝑦2 = −4x2−14y2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 无解．

  2. 求解方程 𝑥2 −41𝑦2 = ±4x2−41y2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

循环节长度 ℓ =5ℓ=5![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为奇数．方程 𝑥2 −41𝑦2 = −4x2−41y2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (𝐺4,𝐵4) =(64,10)(G4,B4)=(64,10)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，方程 𝑥2 −41𝑦2 =4x2−41y2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (𝐺9,𝐵9) =(4098,640)(G9,B9)=(4098,640)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．它们之间有如下关系：

4098+640√412=(64+10√412)2.4098+640412=(64+10412)2.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

当然，因为 𝐷 ≡1(mod8)D≡1(mod8)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，根据前文结论，此时方程 𝑥2 −41𝑦2 = ±4x2−41y2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解一定都是偶数，且总是方程 𝑥2 −41𝑦2 = ±1x2−41y2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解的 22![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 倍，所以也可以直接利用前文的示例得出．

  3. 求解方程 𝑥2 −13𝑦2 = ±4x2−13y2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(1,2,13)(P0,Q0,D)=(1,2,13)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法结果如下：（标红部分为第一个循环节）
