循环节长度 ℓ =1ℓ=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为奇数．方程 𝑥2 −13𝑦2 = −4x2−13y2=−4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (𝐺0,𝐵0) =(3,1)(G0,B0)=(3,1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，方程 𝑥2 −13𝑦2 =4x2−13y2=4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解为 (𝐺1,𝐵1) =(11,3)(G1,B1)=(11,3)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

因为该方程的最小正整数解都是奇数，所以可以利用第三个循环节末尾处的数对 (𝐺2,𝐵2) =(36,10)(G2,B2)=(36,10)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 得到相应的（负）Pell 方程 𝑥2 −13𝑦2 = ±1x2−13y2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解 (18,5)(18,5)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．它也可以通过直接计算得到：

36+10√132=(3+√132)3.36+10132=(3+132)3.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

而且，这是负 Pell 方程的解．相应的 Pell 方程的最小正整数解是 (649,180)(649,180)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

  4. 求解方程 𝑥2 −52𝑦2 = ±4x2−52y2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

因为方程 𝑥2 −13𝑦2 = ±1x2−13y2=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解分别是 (18,5)(18,5)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (649,180)(649,180)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以方程 𝑥2 −52𝑦2 = ±4x2−52y2=±4![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的最小正整数解分别是 (36,10)(36,10)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 (1298,360)(1298,360)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

### 一般情形

最后，讨论广义 Pell 方程的解法．

对于 |𝑁| <√𝐷|N|<D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形有一个简单的解法．前文的结论说明方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 一定满足 𝑥𝑦xy![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 等于 √𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的某个渐近分数．而且，根据前文讨论的解的结构可知，每个基础解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都满足 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 小于等于相应的 Pell 方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =1x2−Dy2=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的基础解 𝑥1 +𝑦1√𝐷x1+y1D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．利用 PQa 算法中分母序列 𝐵𝑘Bk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的单调性可知，广义 Pell 方程的这些基础解一定出现在相应的 Pell 方程的基础解出现之前．由此，只需要对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(0,1,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(0,1,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法，直到 𝑄ℓ′ =1Qℓ′=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 ℓ′ℓ′![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为偶数时为止，过程中对出现的每个 (𝐴𝑘,𝐵𝑘)(Ak,Bk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 检验是否存在整数 𝑓f![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得

𝐴2𝑘−𝐷𝐵2𝑘=(−1)𝑘+1𝑄𝑘+1=𝑁/𝑓2Ak2−DBk2=(−1)k+1Qk+1=N/f2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

成立，如果成立，则记录 (𝑓𝐴𝑘,𝑓𝐵𝑘)(fAk,fBk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是一个最小正整数解．这个过程记录的所有 (𝑓𝐴𝑘,𝑓𝐵𝑘)(fAk,fBk)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的全部最小正整数解．利用 (𝐴ℓ′−1,𝐵ℓ′−1)(Aℓ′−1,Bℓ′−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，即相应的 Pell 方程的基本解，就可以根据求出的这些最小正整数解，生成广义 Pell 方程的所有解．注意，取决于循环节长度 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是偶数还是奇数，上述的 ℓ′ℓ′![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 可能是 ℓℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 或是 2ℓ2ℓ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

对于更为一般的 𝑁N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形，上述方法不再适用．首先，枚举 𝑁N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有平方因子 𝑓2f2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，设 𝑚 =𝑁/𝑓2m=N/f2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，并枚举同余方程 𝑧2 ≡𝐷(mod|𝑚|)z2≡D(mod|m|)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的所有满足 −|𝑚|/2 <𝑧 ≤|𝑚|/2−|m|/2<z≤|m|/2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解 𝑧z![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．然后，对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(𝑧,|𝑚|,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(z,|m|,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法，直到 𝑄𝑘 = ±1Qk=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 或已经结束了一个循环节．在第二种情形，那么与该组 (𝑓,𝑧)(f,z)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 相关的方程的解并不存在．在第一种情形，需要进一步判断 ( −1)𝑘𝑄𝑘 =𝑁/|𝑁|(−1)kQk=N/|N|![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 与否．如果符号一致，那么 (𝑓𝐺𝑘−1,𝑓𝐵𝑘−1)(fGk−1,fBk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．否则，它是方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −𝑁x2−Dy2=−N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，而且当且仅当相应的负 Pell 方程的解存在时，才可以通过复合它与相应的负 Pell 方程的基本解来得到方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解．当完成对所有组 (𝑓,𝑧)(f,z)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的遍历之后，就可以得到方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 在每个解的等价类中各恰好一个解，且该解为该等价类中的基本解或最小正整数解．利用它们和相应的 Pell 方程的基本解，可以生成该方程的所有整数解．这一算法称为 **Lagrange–Matthews–Mollin 算法** ．

该算法的正确性由如下定理保证：

定理

设方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁x2−Dy2=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有整数解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝑥 ≥0,𝑦 >0,gcd(𝑥,𝑦) =1x≥0,y>0,gcd(x,y)=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．令 𝑄0 =|𝑁|Q0=|N|![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，则 gcd(𝑄0,𝑦) =1gcd(Q0,y)=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．设 𝑃0P0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是同余方程 𝑥 ≡ −𝑃0𝑦(mod𝑄0)x≡−P0y(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解且 −𝑄0/2 <𝑃0 ≤𝑄0/2−Q0/2<P0≤Q0/2![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，并设整数 𝑋X![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得 𝑥 =𝑄0𝑋 −𝑃0𝑦x=Q0X−P0y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 成立．那么，𝑃20 ≡𝐷(mod𝑄0)P02≡D(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，𝑋𝑦Xy![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝜔 =𝑃0+√𝐷𝑄0ω=P0+DQ0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的一个渐近分数 𝐴𝑘−1𝐵𝑘−1Ak−1Bk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，且 𝑄𝑘 =( −1)𝑘𝑁|𝑁|Qk=(−1)kN|N|![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

证明

利用 𝑥 ≡ −𝑃0𝑦(mod𝑄0)x≡−P0y(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 =𝑁 ≡0(mod𝑄0)x2−Dy2=N≡0(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，显然有 𝑃20 ≡𝐷(mod𝑄0)P02≡D(modQ0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因而，

𝑃0𝑥+𝐷𝑦≡−𝑃20𝑦+𝐷𝑦=(𝐷−𝑃20)𝑦≡0(mod𝑄0).P0x+Dy≡−P02y+Dy=(D−P02)y≡0(modQ0).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

由此，可以考察整系数矩阵

(𝑃𝑅𝑄𝑆)=⎛⎜ ⎜ ⎜⎝𝑋𝑃0𝑥+𝐷𝑦𝑄0𝑦𝑥⎞⎟ ⎟ ⎟⎠.(PRQS)=(XP0x+DyQ0yx).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

它的行列式

𝑃𝑆−𝑄𝑅=𝑥(𝑥+𝑃0𝑦)−𝑦(𝑃0𝑥+𝐷𝑦)𝑄0=𝑥2−𝐷𝑦2𝑄0=±1.PS−QR=x(x+P0y)−y(P0x+Dy)Q0=x2−Dy2Q0=±1.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

而且，设 𝜁 =√𝐷 >1ζ=D>1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，就有

𝑃𝜁+𝑅𝑄𝜁+𝑆=(𝑥+𝑃0𝑦)√𝐷+(𝑃0𝑥+𝐷𝑦)(𝑥+𝑦√𝐷)𝑄0=𝑃0+√𝐷𝑄0=𝜔.Pζ+RQζ+S=(x+P0y)D+(P0x+Dy)(x+yD)Q0=P0+DQ0=ω.![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

下面要证明 𝑃𝑄PQ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝜔ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的一个渐近分数．不妨设 𝑃𝑄PQ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有 [连分数展开](../continued-fraction/#简单连分数)

𝑃𝑄=[𝑎0,𝑎1,⋯,𝑎𝑘]PQ=[a0,a1,⋯,ak]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

且 𝑃𝑆 −𝑄𝑅 =( −1)𝑘−1PS−QR=(−1)k−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．如果设 𝑝𝑘𝑞𝑘pkqk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是它的第 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个渐近分数，那么 (𝑝𝑘,𝑞𝑘) =(𝑃,𝑄)(pk,qk)=(P,Q)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，且根据 [渐近分数的差分公式](../continued-fraction/#误差估计) 可知，𝑝𝑘𝑞𝑘−1 −𝑞𝑘𝑝𝑘−1 =( −1)𝑘−1pkqk−1−qkpk−1=(−1)k−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．这说明

𝑝𝑘(𝑆−𝑞𝑘−1)=𝑞𝑘(𝑅−𝑝𝑘−1).pk(S−qk−1)=qk(R−pk−1).![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

分情况讨论：

  * 如果 𝑆 =0S=0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么容易验证 𝑄 =𝑅 =1Q=R=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，因而 𝜔 =𝑃 +𝜁−1 =[𝑃,𝜁]ω=P+ζ−1=[P,ζ]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，故而 𝑃𝑄 =𝑃PQ=P![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝜔ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的第 00![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个渐近分数；
  * 如果 𝑄 =𝑆 >0Q=S>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么 𝑄 =𝑆 =1Q=S=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝑃 −𝑅 = ±1P−R=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．此时，
    * 如果 𝑃 =𝑅 +1P=R+1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么 𝜔 =𝑅 +11+𝜁−1 =[𝑅,1,𝜁]ω=R+11+ζ−1=[R,1,ζ]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，故而 𝑃𝑄 =𝑅+11 =[𝑅,1]PQ=R+11=[R,1]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝜔ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的第 11![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个渐近分数；
    * 如果 𝑃 =𝑅 −1P=R−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么 𝜔 =𝑅 −1 +11+𝜁 =[𝑅 −1,𝜁 −1]ω=R−1+11+ζ=[R−1,ζ−1]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，故而 𝑃𝑄 =𝑅 −1PQ=R−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝜔ω![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的第 00![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个渐近分数；
  * 如果 𝑄 ≠𝑆 >0Q≠S>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，那么由于 𝑄 =𝑞𝑘 ∣(𝑆 −𝑞𝑘−1)Q=qk∣(S−qk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，总存在整数 𝜅κ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 使得 𝑆 =𝜅𝑞𝑘 +𝑞𝑘−1S=κqk+qk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 和 𝑅 =𝜅𝑝𝑘 +𝑝𝑘−1R=κpk+pk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 成立．因为 𝑞𝑘 ≥𝑞𝑘−1qk≥qk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝑆 >0S>0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以 𝜅 ≥0κ≥0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因而，𝜔 =(𝜅+𝜁)𝑝𝑘+𝑝𝑘−1(𝜅+𝜁)𝑞𝑘+𝑞𝑘−1 =[𝑎0,𝑎1,⋯,𝑎𝑘,𝜅 +𝜁]ω=(κ+ζ)pk+pk−1(κ+ζ)qk+qk−1=[a0,a1,⋯,ak,κ+ζ]![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，故而 𝑃𝑄PQ![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是它的第 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 个渐近分数．

综上所述，总有 𝑋𝑦Xy![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是 𝜔 =𝑃0+√𝐷𝑄0ω=P0+DQ0![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的渐近分数，并按照 PQa 算法中的记号记作 𝐴𝑘−1𝐵𝑘−1Ak−1Bk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．因为 𝐴2𝑘−1 −𝐷𝐵2𝑘−1 =( −1)𝑘𝑄0𝑄𝑘Ak−12−DBk−12=(−1)kQ0Qk![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以 𝑄𝑘 =( −1)𝑘𝑁|𝑁|Qk=(−1)kN|N|![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

该定理保证了方程的所有正解都存在于相应的二次无理数的渐近分数中．因为利用 PQa 算法计算渐近分数时，只要进入循环节，就一定能保证渐近分数总是正的．所以，只要枚举所有定理条件所允许的二次无理数，计算它的渐近分数直到一个循环节内，就能够找到一个解．因为在同一个二次无理数的渐近分数中出现的两个解，一定是等价的，所以只要得到第一个满足 ( −1)𝑘𝑄𝑘 =𝑁/|𝑁|(−1)kQk=N/|N|![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解，就可以停止继续后面的计算．与前面的所有算法都不同的是，此处满足条件的 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 可能出现在尚未进入循环节时．

示例

  1. 求解方程 𝑥2 −157𝑦2 =12x2−157y2=12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

因为 122 <157122<157![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，所以对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(0,1,157)(P0,Q0,D)=(0,1,157)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法结果如下：（标红部分为第一个循环节）

循环节长度 ℓ =17ℓ=17![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为奇数，所以需要考察两个循环节内 𝐺2𝑘−1 −157𝐵2𝑘−1Gk−12−157Bk−12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 与 1212![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 相差一个平方因子的情形，即 𝑘 =1,9,13,19,23,31k=1,9,13,19,23,31![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的情形．它们对应的解就是下表中的 (𝑓𝐺,𝑓𝐵)(fG,fB)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)：

全体 (𝑓𝐺,𝑓𝐵)(fG,fB)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是方程 𝑥2 −157𝑦2 =12x2−157y2=12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的解集的所有等价类中的最小正整数解．要通过这些解得到全部解，可以利用相应的 Pell 方程的基本解 (46698728731849,3726964292220)(46698728731849,3726964292220)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．比如说，可以将它们转化为该等价类中的基本解 (𝑥,𝑦)(x,y)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，相应的解也一并列于上表中．

  2. 求解方程 𝑥2 −157𝑦2 =12x2−157y2=12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

这次利用 Lagrange–Matthews–Mollin 算法求解．首先，枚举 𝑁 =12N=12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的平方因子：

     * 𝑓2 =12f2=12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，有 𝑚 =12m=12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，同余方程 𝑃2 ≡157(mod12)P2≡157(mod12)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解 𝑧 = ±1, ±5z=±1,±5![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)；
     * 𝑓2 =22f2=22![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，有 𝑚 =3m=3![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，同余方程 𝑃2 ≡157(mod3)P2≡157(mod3)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解 𝑧 = ±1z=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

对于所有可能的 (𝑓,𝑧)(f,z)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 组合运行初始参数为 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(𝑧,|𝑚|,𝐷)(P0,Q0,D)=(z,|m|,D)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的 PQa 算法，并找到首个 ( −1)𝑘𝑄𝑘 =1(−1)kQk=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的位置，对应的 (𝑓𝐺𝑘−1,𝑓𝐵𝑘−1)(fGk−1,fBk−1)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 就是一组解．结果如下表所示：

𝑓f![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑧z![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑚m![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑘k![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑓𝐺𝑘−1fGk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)| 𝑓𝐵𝑘−1fBk−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)

这就是前文列举的所有等价类中的最小正整数解，可以利用 Pell 方程的基本解将它们转化为基本解．

  3. 求解方程 𝑥2 −79𝑦2 = ±101x2−79y2=±101![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

仍然使用 Lagrange–Matthews–Mollin 算法求解．因为 𝑁 =101N=101![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是素数，所以一定有 𝑓 =1f=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．此时，𝑚 =101m=101![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，相应的同余方程 𝑃2 ≡79(mod101)P2≡79(mod101)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解 𝑃 = ±33P=±33![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)．

对 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =(33,101,79)(P0,Q0,D)=(33,101,79)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法结果如下：（标红部分为第一个循环节）

循环节长度 ℓ =6ℓ=6![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 为偶数．直到一个循环节结束，都不存在 𝑄𝑘 = ±1Qk=±1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，因而，该情形无解．相应地，对于 (𝑃0,𝑄0,𝐷) =( −33,101,79)(P0,Q0,D)=(−33,101,79)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 运行 PQa 算法也可以观察到类似的情况．因此，该方程无解．

  * [Solving the diophantine equation x2–Dy2 = N, D > 0 and not a perfect square, N ≠ 0 - Number Theory Web](http://www.numbertheory.org/php/patz.html)（Lagrange–Matthews–Mollin 算法）

* * *

  1. 当 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是完全平方数时，直接做因式分解可知，(𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷)(𝑥 −𝑦√𝐷) =𝑁(x+yD)(x−yD)=N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)，因此所有解可以通过遍历 𝑁N![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的因数得知．特别地，当 𝑁 =1N=1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，方程只有解 ( ±1,0)(±1,0)![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7)；当 𝑁 = −1N=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝐷 ≠1D≠1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 时，方程没有解． ↩

  2. 有些中文文献也称它为第二型 Pell 方程． ↩

  3. 即形如 𝑛 +12n+12![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 且 𝑛 ∈𝐙n∈Z![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的有理数． ↩

  4. 注意，Pell 方程中基本解的定义与实二次整数环中的基本单位数的定义并不一致．首先，部分实二次整数环中的基本单位数 𝑥 +𝑦√𝐷x+yD![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 中的 𝑥,𝑦x,y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 是半整数，因而并非 Pell 方程的解．其次，同一个实二次整数环的基本单位数有四个，但是基本解只有一个，因为基本解要求 𝑥,𝑦x,y![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 都是正数． ↩

  5. 一个较为实用的判断方法和工具在 [这里](http://www.numbertheory.org/php/hardy_williams.html) 及其参考文献．使得方程 𝑥2 −𝐷𝑦2 = −1x2−Dy2=−1![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 有解的正整数 𝐷D![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7) 的列表是 [OEIS A031396](https://oeis.org/A031396)． ↩
